Play area tiles

Click a tile to see the following info:

(x,y)=(10,9)
ref_addr=(x,y+0x98)=A10A
ref=0xDB, udg_page=0x80
udg_addr=(ref,udg_page)=80DB
attr_addr=(x+0x80,y+0x98)=A18A
attr=0x20

where:

  • ref is the UDG reference for the tile (located at ref_addr)
  • udg_page is the base page for the tile graphic data (0x80, 0x88 or 0x90)
  • udg_addr is the base address of the tile graphic data (ref+0100*udg_page)
  • attr is the tile's attribute byte (located at attr_addr)

The base page for the tile graphic data (udg_page) depends on the x-coordinate of the tile as follows:

xudg_page
0-310x80
32-630x88
64-950x90

The eight graphic bytes for a tile are located thus:

AddressContents
(ref,udg_page)=udg_addr Graphic byte 1/8
(ref,udg_page+1)=udg_addr+0100 Graphic byte 2/8
(ref,udg_page+2)=udg_addr+0200 Graphic byte 3/8
(ref,udg_page+3)=udg_addr+0300 Graphic byte 4/8
(ref,udg_page+4)=udg_addr+0400 Graphic byte 5/8
(ref,udg_page+5)=udg_addr+0500 Graphic byte 6/8
(ref,udg_page+6)=udg_addr+0600 Graphic byte 7/8
(ref,udg_page+7)=udg_addr+0700 Graphic byte 8/8

Any given tile (identified by udg_addr) may appear at more than one location in the play area.
